    <div id="action-panel-details" class="action-panel-content yt-uix-expander yt-card yt-card-has-padding yt-uix-expander-collapsed"><div id="watch-description" class="yt-uix-button-panel"><div id="watch-description-content"><div id="watch-description-clip"><div id="watch-uploader-info"><strong class="watch-time-text">Опубликовано: 30 сент. 2015 г.</strong></div><div id="watch-description-text" class=""><p id="eow-description" class="" >sql server row_number example<br />sql server row number by partition<br />sql server row_number over partition by order by<br /><br />In this video we will discuss Row_Number function in SQL Server. This is continuation to Part 108. Please watch Part 108 from SQL Server tutorial before proceeding.<br /><br />Row_Number function<br />Introduced in SQL Server 2005<br />Returns the sequential number of a row starting at 1<br />ORDER BY clause is required<br />PARTITION BY clause is optional<br />When the data is partitioned, row number is reset to 1 when the partition changes<br /><br />Syntax : ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY Col1, Col2) <br /><br />Row_Number function without PARTITION BY : In this example, data is not partitioned, so ROW_NUMBER will provide a consecutive numbering for all the rows in the table based on the order of rows imposed by the ORDER BY clause.<br /><br />SELECT Name, Gender, Salary,     ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY Gender) AS RowNumber<br />FROM Employees<br /><br />Please note : If ORDER BY clause is not specified you will get the following error<br />The function 'ROW_NUMBER' must have an OVER clause with ORDER BY<br /><br />Row_Number function with PARTITION BY : In this example, data is partitioned by Gender, so ROW_NUMBER will provide a consecutive numbering only for the rows with in a parttion. When the partition changes the row number is reset to 1.<br /><br />SELECT Name, Gender, Salary,     ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY Gender ORDER BY Gender) AS RowNumber<br />FROM Employees<br /><br />Use case for Row_Number function : Deleting all duplicate rows except one from a sql server table. <br /><br />Discussed in detail in Part 4 of SQL Server Interview Questions and Answers video series.<br /><br />Link for all dot net and sql server video tutorial playlists<br /><a href="https://www.youtube.com/user/kudvenkat/playlists?sort=dd&amp;view=1" class="yt-uix-sessionlink  " data-sessionlink="itct=CLcBEOk4GAAiEwjygNeanZnSAhUIvhgKHSh2BFco-B0" data-url="https://www.youtube.com/user/kudvenkat/playlists?sort=dd&amp;view=1" >https://www.youtube.com/user/kudvenka...</a><br /><br />Link for slides, code samples and text version of the video<br /><a href="http://csharp-video-tutorials.blogspot.com/2015/09/rownumber-function-in-sql-server.html" class="yt-uix-servicelink  " data-servicelink="CLcBEOk4GAAiEwjygNeanZnSAhUIvhgKHSh2BFco-B0" data-target-new-window="True" data-url="http://csharp-video-tutorials.blogspot.com/2015/09/rownumber-function-in-sql-server.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">http://csharp-video-tutorials.blogspo...</a></p></div>  <div id="watch-description-extras">
    <ul class="watch-extras-section">
